Supply Chain Wizard partners with organizations in designing, developing and implementing digital solutions using state-of-the-art technologies such as Internet-of-Things (IoT), Artificial Intelligence (AI), Machine Learning (ML) and Blockchain through its Cloud Platform to enable end-to-end Digital Supply Chain Transformations in Life Sciences &amp;amp; Pharmaceutical industry. Serving some of the world&amp;#39;s largest pharmaceutical manufacturers, contract manufacturers and packagers, Supply Chain Wizard is dedicated to adding sustainable value through data-driven decision making from Shop Floor to Executive Boardrooms.">

    <section class="core-section-container

<!---->
          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              Supply Chain Wizard, an INC 5000 company, is a management consulting, digital innovation and solutions firm, and a global leader specializing in serialization and traceability, supply chain strategy and operational transformation programs with presence in North America, Latin America, Europe, Middle East and Asia. Supply Chain Wizard partners with organizations in designing, developing and implementing digital solutions using state-of-the-art technologies such as Internet-of-Things (IoT), Artificial Intelligence (AI), Machine Learning (ML) and Blockchain through its Cloud Platform to enable end-to-end Digital Supply Chain Transformations in Life Sciences &amp; Pharmaceutical industry. Serving some of the world's largest pharmaceutical manufacturers, contract manufacturers and packagers, Supply Chain Wizard is dedicated to adding sustainable value through data-driven decision making from Shop Floor to Executive Boardrooms.

In addition to our digital solutions, our consultants are dedicated to supporting clients via trainings, business strategies, and IT implementation.

Our work in serialization (Track &amp; Trace):

•	Leverage industry experts to aid pharma executives in meeting regulatory standards for serialization.

•	Run end-to-end supply chain diagnostics to create customized strategies that provide a healthy ROI

•	Provide Project Management expertise for planning, staffing and execution 


•	Present at major industry conferences to educate on industry best practices
          </p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">We’re excited to share that <a class="link" href="https://de.linkedin.com/in/yigiter-colakoglu?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Yigiter Colakoglu MBA, PMP, PSM</a> and <a class="link" href="https://de.linkedin.com/in/somachhotray?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Soma Chhotray</a> will be representing Supply Chain Wizard at FutureLink Barcelona 2025! 

As a proud <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/tracelink?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>TraceLink</a> partner, we look forward to connecting with industry leaders and innovators from around the world to discuss the future of supply chain, digital transformation, and collaboration.

FutureLink is a fantastic opportunity to share insights, build new relationships, and explore innovative ways to deliver value to our customers and the broader community. We can’t wait to engage with fellow attendees, learn from the best, and help shape the future of our industry.

See you in Barcelona! Interested in joining us? Send us a DM and we’ll be happy to help you with your registration.

Here’s what you’ll walk away with:
- How to future-proof your operations with integrated digital solutions
- The real cost of inaction in the face of changing FDA policies and tariff landscapes
- How top players are turning transformation buzzwords into factory-floor results
- Case studies from the frontlines of digital factory modernization

If you’re tasked with leading change, driving compliance, or hitting digital maturity targets, this is your opportunity to get unstuck and get ahead.

                  <p class="contextual-sign-in-modal__join-now m-auto font-sans text-md text-color-text my-1">
                    LinkedIn‘de yeni misiniz? <a href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww%2Elinkedin%2Ecom%2Fcompany%2Fsupply-chain-wizard-llc&_l=tr&trk=organization_guest_contextual-sign-in-modal_join-link" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_contextual-sign-in-modal_join-link" data-tracking-will-navigate="true" class="contextual-sign-in-modal__join-link">Hemen katılın</a>
                  </p>
                  
    
    
    <p class="linkedin-tc__text text-color-text-low-emphasis text-xs pb-2 contextual-sign-in-modal__terms-and-conditions m-auto w-[320px] pt-2 babybear:w-full" data-impression-id="linkedin-tc__button-skip-tc-text">
      Devam Et seçeneğini tıklayarak veya oturum açarak LinkedIn <a href="/legal/user-agreement?trk=linkedin-tc_auth-button_user-agreement" target="_blank" data-tracking-control-name="linkedin-tc_auth-button_user-agreement" data-tracking-will-navigate="true">Kullanıcı Anlaşması’nı</a>, <a href="/legal/privacy-policy?trk=linkedin-tc_auth-button_privacy-policy" target="_blank" data-tracking-control-name="linkedin-tc_auth-button_privacy-policy" data-tracking-will-navigate="true">Gizlilik Politikası’nı</a> ve <a href="/legal/cookie-policy?trk=linkedin-tc_auth-button_cookie-policy" target="_blank" data-tracking-control-name="linkedin-tc_auth-button_cookie-policy" data-tracking-will-navigate="true">Çerez Politikası’nı</a> kabul etmiş olursunuz.
